# Per-unit validation sources

Evidence artifacts and validation reports for individual algorithm test units.

Return to the [[index|Wiki Index]].

- [[align-global-001-evidence]] — evidence artifact for test unit ALIGN-GLOBAL-001 (Needleman–Wunsch): Wikipedia sources, the `GCATGCG`/`GATTACA` worked example, and the GapExtend-as-*d* / GapOpen-unused note.
- [[align-global-001-report]] — validation report for ALIGN-GLOBAL-001 (Needleman–Wunsch): Stage A/B both PASS, State CLEAN, 13/13 tests green; code path, cross-verification table, and the documented empty-`DnaSequence`-input nuance.
- [[align-local-001-report]] — validation report for ALIGN-LOCAL-001 (Smith–Waterman): Stage A/B both PASS, State CLEAN, 7/7 tests green; hand-recomputed Wikipedia DP matrix (score 13, `GTT-AC`/`GTTGAC`), zero-floor + max-cell + traceback-to-zero code evidence.
- [[align-multi-001-evidence]] — evidence artifact for test unit ALIGN-MULTI-001 (MSA): main doc + MUSCLE and T-Coffee addenda; star/iterative/consistency aligners, SP-score and consensus design choices.
- [[align-multi-001-report]] — validation report for ALIGN-MULTI-001 (MSA, full re-validation): Stage A/B both PASS, State CLEAN, 96 family tests green (suite 18208/0); re-confirms star + progressive (UPGMA) + consistency (T-Coffee), with probe-verified GARFIELD relation (primary 200 → extended 375) and the summed-vs-averaged group-column divergence carried as a design assumption.
- [[align-semi-001-evidence]] — evidence artifact for test unit ALIGN-SEMI-001 (semi-global / fitting): Wikipedia + Rosalind SIMS/SMGB + Brudno 2003 sources, fitting-variant init/traceback, INV-1..5.
- [[align-semi-001-report]] — validation report for ALIGN-SEMI-001 (semi-global / fitting): Stage A/B both PASS, State CLEAN, 17 canonical + property tests green; hand-recomputed fitting cases (M1 4, GAP 2, MIX 1, MAX 3 = max-of-last-row not bottom-right), 11/11 cross-verification table, first-row-0 / no-zero-floor / argmax-last-row code evidence.
- [[align-stats-001-evidence]] — evidence artifact for test unit ALIGN-STATS-001 (identity/similarity/gaps + srspair formatting): EMBOSS needle/AlignFormats + BLAST + pseqsid sources, denominator-includes-gaps rule, three datasets.
- [[align-stats-001-report]] — validation report for ALIGN-STATS-001 (identity/similarity/gaps + formatting): Stage A/B both PASS-WITH-NOTES, State CLEAN, suite 6536/0; re-derived EMBOSS 65/90/9 → 43.6/60.4/6.0%, 7/7 cross-verification table, O(L)-column-classify + `score.Mismatch>0` similarity code evidence; sole note is the rendering-only srspair `:`/`.` display simplification.
- [[annot-coding-001-evidence]] — evidence artifact for test unit ANNOT-CODING-001 (CPAT hexamer coding-potential score): CPAT paper + FrameKmer.py + EMBOSS tcode sources, mean-ln-ratio formula, ±1 pseudo-scores, worked example 0.3466.
- [[annot-coding-001-report]] — validation report for ANNOT-CODING-001 (CPAT hexamer coding-potential score): Stage A PASS-WITH-NOTES / Stage B PASS-after-fix, State CLEAN, suite 6561/0; found+fixed a real defect (both-zero hexamer counted instead of skipped) in code + a code-echo test C1 (0.6931→1.3863) + 3 docs; re-anchored C1 to canonical FrameKmer.py.
- [[annot-codonusage-001-evidence]] — evidence artifact for test unit ANNOT-CODONUSAGE-001 (RSCU): LIRMM + PMC2528880 + Sharp & Li 1986 + CodonU sources, n_i·x/Σx formula, Leu 3/1.5/1.5/0/0/0 example, pooled-counts + sense-codons-only, no CAI pseudocount.
- [[annot-codonusage-001-report]] — validation report for ANNOT-CODONUSAGE-001 (RSCU, GenomeAnnotator.GetCodonUsage): Stage A PASS / Stage B PASS-WITH-NOTES, State CLEAN, suite 6568/0; no code defect, formula confirmed verbatim (LIRMM/cubar), closed 3 test-coverage gaps (Trp single-codon, 61-sense-codon set, empty-enumerable branch), zero code change.
- [[annot-gene-001-report]] — validation report for ANNOT-GENE-001 (prokaryotic gene prediction + Shine-Dalgarno RBS detection, GenomeAnnotator.PredictGenes / FindRibosomeBindingSitesBothStrands): Stage A/B both PASS, State CLEAN, filtered suite 39/0; independent re-validation, no defect — SD consensus AGGAGG / anti-SD YACCUCCUUA / 5 nt optimal spacing confirmed and the reverse-strand mapping `forwardPos = len − revPos − motifLen` hand-re-derived + mutation-falsified (R1/R3/R4), zero code change.
- [[annot-gff-001-report]] — validation report for ANNOT-GFF-001 (annotation-layer GFF3 I/O, GenomeAnnotator.ToGff3 / ParseGff3 — distinct from FileIO GffParser / [[parse-gff-001-evidence]]): Stage A/B both PASS, State CLEAN, GFF3 fixture 46/46, full suite 18783/0; fresh re-validation of the export-fidelity fix (real source/score cols + per-transcript cumulative CDS phase `(3 − Σ preceding mod 3) mod 3`, 5′→3′ ordering descending on `−`) against SO GFF3 v1.26, hand-recomputed phases 0,1,1 / 0,0,0,0 / minus-strand 2,2,0, zero code change.
- [[annot-orf-001-report]] — validation report for ANNOT-ORF-001 (annotation-layer ORF detection, GenomeAnnotator.FindOrfs / FindLongestOrfsPerFrame — distinct from the ATG-only GenomicAnalyzer unit [[genomic-orf-001-evidence]]): Stage A PASS / Stage B PASS-WITH-NOTES, End state CLEAN, ORF filter 35/0, full suite 18208/0; no defect — start set ATG+GTG/TTG, stops TAA/TAG/TGA, six frames, `minLength` in amino acids, stop-inclusive coords all confirmed vs Rosalind (live) / Wikipedia / NCBI ORFfinder / Deonier 2005 / Claverie 1997, Rosalind four-protein sample reproduced (incl. reverse-strand protein) + nested shared-stop ORF verified in-code, zero code change; sole note is the non-canonical `requireStartCodon=false` run-off seeding path.
- [[annot-prom-001-report]] — validation report for ANNOT-PROM-001 (prokaryotic promoter motif detection, `GenomeAnnotator.FindPromoterMotifs` — the scored −10/−35 detector, distinct from the `GenomicAnalyzer.FindMotif` catalog scan [[regulatory-element-detection]]): Stage A/B both PASS, End state CLEAN, promoter-motif filter 20/0 (28 cases), zero code change; −35 `TTGACA` / −10 `TATAAT` consensus, E. coli per-position probabilities (sums 373 / 412), score = Σ matched-p / Σ all-6-p ∈ [0,1] all confirmed vs Wikipedia Promoter-genetics / Pribnow-box (live) + Pribnow 1975 / Harley & Reynolds 1987, all 8 partial-variant scores hand-recomputed (prefix-5/suffix-5/prefix-4, e.g. `TTGAC` 0.855 / `ATAAT` 0.813); declared scope limits (17 bp spacing NOT enforced, exact-substring not PWM), `position` is a 0-based string index not the TSS-relative coordinate. Concept [[promoter-detection]].
- [[annot-repeat-001-evidence]] — evidence artifact for test unit ANNOT-REPEAT-001 (repeat detection/classification): Wikipedia + IUPACpal + RepeatMasker sources; tandem/inverted/gapped-IR + repeat-class vocab; exact-substring-not-Smith-Waterman ClassifyRepeat assumption.
- [[annot-repeat-001-report]] — validation report for ANNOT-REPEAT-001 (repetitive element detection & classification, GenomeAnnotator.FindRepetitiveElements / ClassifyRepeat — distinct from the evidence artifact [[annot-repeat-001-evidence]]): Stage A/B both PASS, End state CLEAN, full suite 6566/0, ledger row 58 / finding A17; one real defect found and fully fixed — `ClassifyRepeat` bidirectional containment (`query.Contains(element) || element.Contains(query)`) misclassified a 1-bp query `"A"`→`"SINE/Alu"` because a longer consensus contained its letters, made one-directional (`element ⊆ query`, RepeatMasker screen-query-for-elements model) + M7b/M7c/M5b/M6b/INV-3 tests added; tandem head-to-tail ≥2 copies / primitive-unit, IR `W G W̄ᴿ` gap-0-palindrome + hand-checked revcomps, RepeatMasker class vocab all confirmed vs Wikipedia + NIH glossary + IUPACpal (Hampson 2021) + RepeatMasker. Concept [[repetitive-element-detection]].
- [[assembly-consensus-001-evidence]] — evidence artifact for test unit ASSEMBLY-CONSENSUS-001 (column-wise consensus): Biopython dumb_consensus + EMBOSS cons + Wikipedia sources; threshold/tie→ambiguous/gap-skip decision rule; default N-not-X and 0.5-not-0.7 assumptions.
- [[assembly-consensus-001-report]] — validation report for ASSEMBLY-CONSENSUS-001 (consensus computation, `SequenceAssembler.ComputeConsensus`; the **C** of OLC — distinct from the evidence artifact [[assembly-consensus-001-evidence]]): Stage A 🟡 PASS-WITH-NOTES / Stage B ✅ PASS / State CLEAN, full suite 6532/0, zero code or test change. Validator re-ran the **Biopython 1.85** `dumb_consensus` reference on all datasets — 10/10 match (M1 `ACGT`, M3 `NC`, M4 `N`, M7 `ANT`, C1 `X` …) — confirming the predicate `unique-max ∧ num_atoms>0 ∧ max_size/num_atoms ≥ threshold else ambiguous` (gaps `{-,.}` skipped, all-gap short-circuits div-by-zero, length = longest read) maps 1:1 to code (`SequenceAssembler.cs:861-926`). The two notes are parameter-reachable **default divergences** from Biopython (threshold 0.5-not-0.7, ambiguous `N`-not-`X`); `require_multiple` intentionally unimplemented. Concept [[consensus-sequence]].
- [[assembly-correct-001-evidence]] — evidence artifact for test unit ASSEMBLY-CORRECT-001 (two-sided k-mer-spectrum read error correction): Musket + Quake + solid-k-mer sources; trusted/untrusted rule, ambiguity→unchanged, k=3/k=1 worked examples; non-behavioral kmerSize=15/minKmerFrequency=2 defaults.
- [[assembly-correct-001-report]] — validation report for ASSEMBLY-CORRECT-001 (k-mer spectrum two-sided read error correction, `SequenceAssembler.ErrorCorrectReads`; distinct from the evidence artifact [[assembly-correct-001-evidence]]): Stage A 🟡 PASS-WITH-NOTES / Stage B ✅ PASS / State CLEAN, full suite 6535/0. Sourced verbatim to Musket + Quake + SAP/EULER + solid-k-mer; validator's Python reimplementation reproduced M1/M2/M3/S1/S2/C1/C2 exactly (k=3 → unique correction to A). One code-echoing test (M4, defect A22) rewritten to a genuine no-valid-correction case (`AAAAAAAA`×3 + `AACCAAAA`, k=4 → unchanged); no algorithm defect. Two carried notes: all-covering vs Musket's leftmost+rightmost, and `≥` vs `>` threshold. Concept [[kmer-spectrum-error-correction]].
- [[assembly-cover-001-evidence]] — evidence artifact for test unit ASSEMBLY-COVER-001 (per-base coverage/depth): Illumina + Daniel Cook + Metagenomics Wiki + Lander-Waterman sources; depth/average/breadth definitions, ACGTTGCAAT worked example (1.5/1.0), e^−c gap/breadth Poisson check; placement-out-of-scope assumption.
- [[assembly-cover-001-report]] — validation report for ASSEMBLY-COVER-001 (coverage/depth, `SequenceAssembler.CalculateCoverage`→`int[]`; distinct from the evidence artifact [[assembly-cover-001-evidence]]): Stage A 🟡 PASS-WITH-NOTES / Stage B ✅ PASS / State CLEAN, full suite 6532→6533/0, zero code change. `depth[i]=#reads spanning i`, `avg=Σ/G`, `breadth=covered/G` matched verbatim to Metagenomics Wiki/Cook/Illumina; C=LN/G (5·3/10=1.5) cross-checks Σdepth/G on ACGTTGCAAT `[1,1,1,2,2,2,2,2,1,1]`. Carried note: the `min(pos+L,refLen)` boundary clip is **dead/defensive** — `FindBestAlignment` places reads only where they fit entirely, so the overhang partial-contribution case is unreachable. Fixed one test gap (empty reference → `[]`). Concept [[coverage-depth-calculation]].
- [[assembly-dbg-001-evidence]] — evidence artifact for test unit ASSEMBLY-DBG-001 (de Bruijn graph assembly): Langmead notes + Jones & Pevzner (Euler theorems 8.1/8.2) + Compeau-Pevzner-Tesler 2011 sources; (k-1)-mer node/edge construction, Eulerian-walk spelling rule, AAABBBA/a_long…/to_every…/ATGGCGTGCA oracles; multiple-walk/gap/error failure modes; walk-selection + empty + short-read assumptions.
- [[assembly-dbg-001-report]] — validation report for ASSEMBLY-DBG-001 (de Bruijn graph assembly, `SequenceAssembler.BuildDeBruijnGraph` + `AssembleDeBruijn`; distinct from the evidence artifact [[assembly-dbg-001-evidence]]): Stage A ✅ PASS / Stage B 🟡 PASS-WITH-NOTES / State CLEAN, full suite 6497/0, zero code change. Chop bound `i∈[0,|r|−k]`, prefix/suffix split, multimap multiedge, and Hierholzer spelling matched verbatim to Langmead + J&P Thm 8.1/8.2; independent Python Hierholzer reproduced AAABBBA/a_long…/to_every…/ATGGCGTGCA + the AAABBBBA multiedge. Only issue a test-coverage gap (three untested-but-documented branches: disconnected-graph one-contig-per-component, `MinContigLength` filter, `BuildDeBruijnGraph(null)` guard), closed with three exact-value tests. Concept [[de-bruijn-graph-assembly]].
- [[assembly-merge-001-evidence]] — evidence artifact for test unit ASSEMBLY-MERGE-001 (contig merging / suffix–prefix overlap collapse): Langmead SCS + OLC + MIT 7.91J sources; overlap = suffix-of-X/prefix-of-Y, `MergeContigs` collapse arithmetic |m|=|c1|+|c2|−l, BAAB/AAABBBA/plain-concat oracles; trusted-length + out-of-range→concatenate API-contract assumptions.
- [[assembly-merge-001-report]] — validation report for ASSEMBLY-MERGE-001 (contig merging, `SequenceAssembler.MergeContigs(c1,c2,overlapLength)`; distinct from the evidence artifact [[assembly-merge-001-evidence]]): Stage A ✅ PASS / Stage B ✅ PASS / State CLEAN, full suite 6529/0, zero code change. Merge path `c1 + c2.Substring(l)` = `X+Y[l:]`, `|merge|=|c1|+|c2|−l`; single fallback covers `l≤0` and `l>min(|c1|,|c2|)` → plain concat, matching the `suffixPrefixMatch` guard; null → `ArgumentNullException`. Independent Python re-impl reproduced BAAB/AAABBBA (exact Langmead strings) + ACGT+CGTAA→ACGTAA, GATTACA+ACATGAA→GATTACATGAA; all 12 tests exact-value, HARD gate PASS, no defect. Concept [[contig-merge-overlap-collapse]].
- [[assembly-olc-001-evidence]] — evidence artifact for test unit ASSEMBLY-OLC-001 (Overlap-Layout-Consensus): Compeau/Pevzner/Tesler 2011 + Langmead OLC/SCS sources; overlap graph + Hamiltonian-path (NP-complete) layout + majority consensus; GTACGTACGAT 12-edge / 5-overlap-tiling / CTCTAGGCC oracles; identity-1.0 + empty-input assumptions.
- [[assembly-olc-001-report]] — validation report for ASSEMBLY-OLC-001 (Overlap-Layout-Consensus, `SequenceAssembler.AssembleOLC` + `FindAllOverlaps` (+cancellable) + `FindOverlap`; distinct from the evidence artifact [[assembly-olc-001-evidence]]): Stage A ✅ PASS / Stage B 🟡 PASS-WITH-NOTES / State CLEAN, full suite 6494/0, zero code change. Longest-suffix-prefix realised by descending scan (pos1=len1−L, pos2=0), case-insensitive identity fraction, no self-overlaps; greedy best-successor layout = superstring merge. Independent Python re-derived the 12-edge GTACGTACGAT set {4,5}, CTCTAGGCC/TAGGCCCTC len 6, chain→`AAAAACCCCCGGGGGTTTTT`, 7/8 identity gate, minOverlap boundary. PASS-WITH-NOTES = two sourced intentional simplifications (greedy vs Hamiltonian-optimal; concatenation vs majority consensus). Only issue a test-coverage gap (`MinContigLength` discard branch), closed with exact-value test M5b. Concept [[overlap-layout-consensus-assembly]].
- [[assembly-scaffold-001-evidence]] — evidence artifact for test unit ASSEMBLY-SCAFFOLD-001 (scaffolding): ABySS 2.0 + NCBI AGP v2.1 + Sahlin 2012 + Bambus sources; scaffold = ordered contigs interspersed with `N`-runs = distance estimate, non-positive gap → AGP unknown-size default 100 N; ACGTNNNTTGGNNCCAA / AAAA+100N+TTTT oracles; source-backed-100-constant scoping assumption.
- [[assembly-scaffold-001-report]] — validation report for ASSEMBLY-SCAFFOLD-001 (scaffolding, `SequenceAssembler.Scaffold(contigs, links, gapCharacter='N')`; distinct from the evidence artifact [[assembly-scaffold-001-evidence]]): Stage A ✅ PASS / Stage B ✅ PASS / State CLEAN, full suite 6529→6531/0, zero production-code change. Gap rule `gapLength = gapSize>0 ? gapSize : UnknownGapLength(100)` (line 733) = INV-01/02; path-follow appends `gapChar`×gapLength then next contig (concatenate-with-N-run, Jackman verbatim); `used` HashSet = one-scaffold-per-contig, unreached → length-1 scaffold ascending. Hand cross-check reproduced `ACGTNNNTTGGNNCCAA` (17), `AAAA`+100N+`TTTT` (108), gap-0→100N. HARD gate PASS (M3/M4 lock exactly 100 N, defeating a wrong `Math.Max(1,gapSize)`); closed two branch-coverage gaps (successor-already-placed → `AANNCCNNNGG`; multi-forward-link first-declared tie-break → `["AANNCC","GG"]`). No defect; sourced simplifications (link ranking / overlap resolution / orientation) out of scope. Concept [[scaffolding]].
- [[assembly-stats-001-evidence]] — evidence artifact for test unit ASSEMBLY-STATS-001 (assembly statistics N50/L50/Nx/auN): Miller 2010 + Wikipedia + QUAST `N50.py` + Heng Li 2020 sources; largest-first inclusive-≥ threshold, auN=ΣL²/ΣL; Assembly A {80,70,50,40,30,20}→N50 70/L50 2, Assembly B→N50 50/L50 3, auN 73.333 oracles; empty→zeros + upper-median-not-source-derived assumptions.
- [[assembly-stats-001-report]] — validation report for ASSEMBLY-STATS-001 (assembly statistics, `GenomeAssemblyAnalyzer.CalculateStatistics`/`CalculateNx`/`CalculateN50`/`CalculateAuN`/`FindGaps`; distinct from the evidence artifact [[assembly-stats-001-evidence]]): Stage A ✅ PASS / Stage B ✅ PASS / State CLEAN / test-quality PASS, full suite 6497/0, zero code or test change. Inclusive Nx boundary proven equal to QUAST `s<=limit` via `cumulative*100 >= totalLength*threshold` (long accum, no overflow); auN=Σl²/Σl; `FindGaps` 0-based inclusive `[Start,End]` maximal N-runs + minGap filter. Hand cross-check reproduced A→70/2, N90 30/5, auN 57.586, B→50/3, {50,50}→50/1 inclusive, minGap-5 filter. 23 tests, exact `Is.EqualTo`/`Within(1e-10)`, no green-washing. Non-defect notes: `CalculateNxCurve` wrapper + `MedianLength` upper-median (Assumption 2), empty→zeros vs QUAST `None` (Assumption 1). Concept [[assembly-statistics]].
- [[assembly-trim-001-evidence]] — evidence artifact for test unit ASSEMBLY-TRIM-001 (quality trimming, BWA/cutadapt running-sum): cutadapt algorithm docs + BWA `bwa_trim_read`/`BWA_MIN_RDLEN` + Cock et al. 2010 sources; subtract-cutoff/argmin-partial-sum = BWA argmax, Phred+33 decode; `KI;<)(,%#$`@thr 10→first 4 bases oracle; both-end-order + minLength-filter assumptions.
- [[assembly-trim-001-report]] — validation report for ASSEMBLY-TRIM-001 (quality trimming, `SequenceAssembler.QualityTrimReads`/`TrimEnd`/`TrimStart`; distinct from the evidence artifact [[assembly-trim-001-evidence]]): Stage A ✅ PASS / Stage B ❌ FAIL → 🔧 FIXED / State CLEAN, full suite 6535/0. **One real defect fully fixed** — old `TrimEnd`/`TrimStart` took the *global-minimum* partial sum with **no `s < 0` early break** and chained the 5' pass onto the 3'-surviving window; ~19.5% of random reads diverged from cutadapt (`20,0,8,40`@10 kept only the last base vs all 4). Fix adds the `s<0` early break to both passes, runs each independently over the full read `[0,n)`, and adds the `start≥stop ⇒ (0,0)` drop rule; Python port vs cutadapt `quality_trim_index` = **0/900k mismatches**. Three new sourced tests (`5!)I`→`ACGT`, `##I##`→`G`, `5&&`→dropped) each fail the old code. Pre-existing M1–M5/S1–S3 were all happy-path and shared the blind spot. Corrected the concept's stale "5'-pass-on-surviving-window" wording. Concept [[quality-trimming-running-sum]].
- [[chrom-aneu-001-evidence]] — evidence artifact for test unit CHROM-ANEU-001 (aneuploidy detection): first Chromosome-analysis file; Wikipedia Aneuploidy/CNV + Griffiths + Santaguida-Amon + McCarroll-Altshuler sources; log2 depth-ratio → CN=round(2^logRatio×2) clamped [0,10], ≥80%-bin whole-chromosome call, confidence=1−min(1,|CN/2−2^logRatio|); Down/Edwards/Patau/Turner/Klinefelter oracles; sex-chromosome + partial-aneuploidy limitations.
- [[chrom-aneu-001-report]] — validation report for CHROM-ANEU-001 (aneuploidy detection, `ChromosomeAnalyzer.DetectAneuploidy` / `IdentifyWholeChromosomeAneuploidy`, `ChromosomeAnalyzer.cs:832–917`, type `CopyNumberState`; distinct from the evidence artifact [[chrom-aneu-001-evidence]]): Stage A PASS / Stage B PASS / End state CLEAN, 31 passed 0 failed, build 0w/0e, zero code or test change. Independent Wikipedia "Aneuploidy" confirmation (ladder + Down/Turner/Edwards/Patau oracles); hand cross-check at medianDepth=30 (0/15/30/45/60 → CN 0/1/2/3/4, confidence 1.0) reproduced against code; `Math.Pow(2,Math.Log2(x))==x` so CN=round((mean/median)×2), CN=2 excluded; clamp 10×→CN 10 / 0.01×→CN 0; log-ratio asserts include `double.NegativeInfinity`. Boundary vs CHROM-KARYO-001 (`AnalyzeKaryotype`+static `GetAneuploidyTerm` labeling vs read-depth→CN call) — no overlap conflict; cosmetic CN>5 label diff ("Polysomy (N)" vs "Copy number = N") not a defect. Accepted limitation: sex chromosomes not baseline-adjusted. Concept [[aneuploidy-detection]].

Boundary vs CHROM-ANEU-001: sibling `IdentifyWholeChromosomeAneuploidy` hardcodes a diploid baseline (`CopyNumber!=2`) — correct for ANEU, not a KARYO divergence. Findings none. Concept [[karyotype-analysis]].
- [[chrom-synt-001-evidence]] — evidence artifact for test unit CHROM-SYNT-001 (synteny analysis): fourth Chromosome-analysis file; Wikipedia Synteny/Comparative-genomics/Rearrangement + MCScanX/SyRI/MUMmer sources; `FindSyntenyBlocks` (ortholog pairs grouped by chr pair → collinear runs merged under maxGap, ≥minGenes; I1–I5 incl. - [[chrom-telo-001-evidence]] — evidence artifact for test unit CHROM-TELO-001 (telomere analysis): fifth Chromosome-analysis file; Wikipedia Telomere + Meyne 1989 (TTAGGG conserved) + Cawthon 2002 (T/S ratio) + Blackburn-Gall 1978 sources; 3′ TTAGGG / 5′ CCCTAA end detection, 70%-per-window purity (5/6 or 5/7 match), T/S linearity length=refLen×(tsRatio/refRatio), IsCriticallyShort=(hasTelomere&&len<criticalLen)OR empty; 1200-bp/purity-0.833/12000/searchLen-truncation + T/S oracles; criticalLength/minTelomereLength/searchLength/referenceLength are configurable defaults not biological constants; deviations None.
- [[chrom-telo-001-report]] — validation report for CHROM-TELO-001 (telomere analysis, `ChromosomeAnalyzer.AnalyzeTelomeres(name, sequence, telomereRepeat="TTAGGG", searchLength=10000, minTelomereLength=500, criticalLength=3000)` + `EstimateTelomereLengthFromTSRatio(tsRatio, referenceRatio=1.0, referenceLength=7000)` + constant `HumanTelomereRepeat="TTAGGG"`, `ChromosomeAnalyzer.cs:250–352`; distinct from the evidence artifact [[chrom-telo-001-evidence]]): validated 2026-06-24, Stage A PASS / Stage B PASS / End state ✅ CLEAN, build 0 warnings/errors, 33 Telomere tests pass, zero code change. TTAGGG (Moyzis 1988 / Meyne 1989, 91 vertebrate species) + CCCTAA reverse-complement 5′ strand + Cawthon 2002 T/S proportionality confirmed against first-sources; 3′=forward TTAGGG backward from terminus / 5′=CCCTAA forward from start, contiguous-tandem-till-<0.7-similarity counting (internal motif not counted), length=windows×repeatLen, purity=match/total, T/S=refLen×(tsRatio/refRatio). Independent hand cross-check reproduced 1200/purity-1.0, divergent TTAGGA→5/6, searchLen-600→600 truncation, T/S {1.5,0.5,2.0,1@ref2,0}→{10500,3500,14000,3500,0}. Findings none; in-spec note: 3′ scan phase-anchored to the terminus (assumes run ends at sequence end); criticalLength/minTelomereLength/searchLength/referenceLength are configurable defaults not biological constants. - [[trans-sixframe-001-evidence]] — evidence artifact for test unit TRANS-SIXFRAME-001 (**six-frame translation** + **START→STOP ORF finding**, the same `Translator` surface as TRANS-PROT-001, from the reference-implementation angle): **Biopython `six_frame_translations`** (governing algorithm) + **EMBOSS `transeq`** (frame values 1/2/3/F/−1/−2/−3/R/6) + **EMBOSS `getorf`** (`-find 1` START→STOP model) + **NCBI transl_table=1** + **Wikipedia Reading-frame** sources. Key distinctive detail: the **reverse-frame numbering convention** — this repo uses the **Biopython independent-offset** rule (frame −k = reverse-complement translated 5'→3' at offset k−1, no correspondence to +1), the documented "alternative" to EMBOSS's phase-locked default (hence `ACTGG` frame −1 = `P` here vs `S` in EMBOSS — a labelling convention, not a bug). ORF `FindOrfs` = START→STOP, start-residue included / stop excluded, `minLength` in **amino acids** (getorf's `-minsize` is nucleotides). Oracles: 39-nt full six-frame table; `GGGATGAAACCCTAAGGG` → `MKP` (start 3, end 14 incl.). **Enriched** [[genetic-code-translation]] (no new concept); genetic-code-parameterized sibling of ATG-only [[open-reading-frame-detection]].

- [[protmotif-sp-001-evidence]] — evidence artifact for test unit PROTMOTIF-SP-001 (signal-peptide cleavage-site prediction, `ProteinMotifFinder.PredictSignalPeptide`; ProteinMotif family): **redesign of the SAME method** — **replaces** the fabricated tripartite n/h/c model of [[protmotif-domain-001-evidence|DOMAIN-001]] with the **von Heijne (1986) log-odds weight matrix** = EMBOSS 6.6.0 `sigcleave` (doc + `sigcleave.c` + `data/Esig.euk`/`Esig.pro`). Score = argmax over sites of `Σ ln(count/expect)` across positions −13..+2 (natural log; zero counts → `1.0e-10` at conserved cols −3/−1, else `1.0`); cleavage between −1/+1, `CleavagePosition` = 1-based mature start; `IsLikelySignalPeptide ⇔ Score ≥ 3.5` (`minWeight` default 3.5, ~95% sens/spec, cleavage 75–80% correct); eukaryotic matrix (161 seqs) default, prokaryotic (36 seqs) via `prokaryote:true`. Worked oracle **ACH2_DROME (UniProt P17644)** → Score **13.739**, mature start **42**, window `LLVLLLLCETVQA` (re-derived exactly in Python). Corner cases: best site always reported (`minWeight` only flags likelihood); < 15-aa window → null; non-standard residues contribute 0; case-insensitive. One assumption (min length = 15-aa window); pitfalls log10-vs-ln and missing −3/−1 penalty. Enriches [[protein-domain-and-signal-peptide-prediction]] (no new concept).

- [[kmer-unique-001-evidence]] — evidence artifact for test unit KMER-UNIQUE-001 (Unique / singleton k-mers + min-count frequency filtering, `KmerAnalyzer.FindUniqueKmers` + `FindKmersWithMinCount`; seventh K-mer family Evidence): Wikipedia K-mer (L−k+1 total, AGAT example) + BioInfoLogics (total/distinct/**unique**="appear only once", ATCGATCAC k=3 → 7/6/5) + Compeau & Pevzner (`Count(Text,Pattern)` overlapping occurrences, most-frequent / `Count≥t` recurrent) sources; `FindUniqueKmers`=Count==1 singletons, `FindKmersWithMinCount`=Count≥minCount ordered by count desc; ATCGATCAC k=3→{TCG,CGA,GAT,TCA,CAC} (ATC=2 excluded) + AGAT k=2→{AG,GA,AT} + ACGTACGT k=4 (ACGT=2) FindKmersWithMinCount(…,2)→{(ACGT,2)}/(…,1)→all-4-desc/FindUniqueKmers→{CGTA,GTAC,TACG} + AAAAA k=3→∅ oracles; empty/k>L→empty, k≤0→ArgumentOutOfRangeException, case-insensitive corner cases; two assumptions (minCount≤1→all distinct count-desc, upper-casing); no contradictions. Synthesized in [[unique-and-mincount-kmers]]; clarifies the singleton-vs-distinct distinction vs [[k-mer-statistics]].

- [[onco-driver-001-evidence]] — evidence artifact for test unit ONCO-DRIVER-001 (Driver Mutation Detection, the Vogelstein 2013 20/20 rule; twelfth Oncology unit): Vogelstein 2013 Science "Cancer Genome Landscapes" (originating source; oncogene = >20% recurrent-position missense/activating, TSG = >20% inactivating/truncating; lenient; IDH1 codon-132 → oncogene) + Tokheim & Karchin 2020 (20/20+, verbatim rule, inactivating = nonsense/frameshift) + Schroeder 2014 OncodriveROLE (truncating list = frameshift/gained-or-lost-stop/splice donor-acceptor; writes "≥20%") + Miller 2017 (recurrent position = same position ≥2×, IDH1 R132H codon 132) sources; methods `IdentifyDriverMutations`/`MatchCancerHotspots`(caller-supplied hotspot set)/`ScoreDriverPotential`(=max of the two criterion fractions in [0,1]; CADD/SIFT/PolyPhen caller-supplied, not implemented); oracles IDH1 10 missense@codon132 → recurrent-missense 1.00 → Oncogene, 8/10 truncating → 0.80 → TumorSuppressor, truncating exactly 0.20 → NOT TSG (strict `>`), neither → Ambiguous; three assumptions (strict `>0.20`, dual-pass tie-break by larger fraction/Ambiguous on tie, ScoreDriverPotential proxy); heuristic not a statistical test (20/20+/MutSigCV out of scope); no contradictions (sole ≥/> glyph resolved to strict). - [[onco-hetero-001-evidence]] — evidence artifact for test unit ONCO-HETERO-001 (Tumor Heterogeneity Analysis — MATH score + Shannon clonal diversity + subclone count + subclonal fraction; seventeenth Oncology unit, the scalar-summary ITH-metric layer): Mroz & Rocco 2013 *Oral Oncology* (rank 1, verbatim **MATH = 100·MAD/median** of the mutant-allele-fraction distribution) + Mroz 2015 *PLOS Medicine* (rank 1, the **1.4826** MAD→SD scaling + full procedure) + maftools `mathScore.R` (rank 3, byte-identical `median(abs(vaf−median vaf))·100·1.4826/median(vaf)`, /100 rescale only if max>1) + Liu & Zhang 2017 *BMC Genomics* PMC5468233 (rank 1, **Shannon S = −Σ pᵢ ln pᵢ** natural-log over clone fractions, richness = #clones) + Shannon 1948 (rank 4 corroborating) + Landau 2013 (reused CCF<0.95 clonal threshold for subclonal fraction) sources; MATH odd {0.10..0.50}→**49.42** / even {0.20..0.80}→**59.304**, Shannon {1.0}→0 / {0.5,0.5}→ln2=0.6931 / four-equal→ln4=1.3863 oracles; zero-median-VAF→undefined/throw, all-identical or single mutation MAD=0→MATH=0, single clone H=0 corner cases; two source-consistent assumptions (Shannon pᵢ = per-CCF-cluster mutation proportions; R even-count median); no contradictions. - [[onco-purity-001-evidence]] — evidence artifact for test unit ONCO-PURITY-001 (Tumor Purity Estimation from somatic SNV VAF / allele-specific copy number; twenty-eighth Oncology unit): CNAqc vignette + Genome Biology 2024 (Antonello, doi:10.1186/s13059-024-03170-5, rank 1/3) verbatim expected-VAF formula `v = m·π·c/[2(1−π)+π(n_A+n_B)]` (m=multiplicity, π=purity, c=clonality; denominator = normal diploid `2(1−π)` + tumour `π·n_tot`), worked examples purity 60%→VAF 30% (v=π/2, π=2·VAF) + 2:1 segment two clonal peaks 33%/66% (m=1/2, n_tot=3, π=1) + FACETS Shen & Seshan NAR 2016 (rank 1, mixing model `m*=mΦ+(1−Φ)` confirms the denominator) + ABSOLUTE Carter 2012 Nat Biotechnol (rank 1, inverse allelic-fraction→multiplicity correction) sources; oracles VAF 0.30→π 0.60, band 0.55–0.65↔VAF 0.275–0.325, 2:1 v=1/3 & 2/3 both→π 1; corner cases multiplicity ambiguity on amplified segments, subclonal c<1 depresses VAF (underestimates purity), purity <0.1 below detection; two assumptions (copy-neutral-diploid default for `EstimatePurityFromVAF`, median cross-variant aggregation); no contradictions. Own concept [[tumor-purity-from-mutation-vaf]] (`alternative_to` the ONCO-ASCAT-001 joint grid fit [[allele-specific-copy-number-ascat]] — closed-form VAF inversion, not a logR/BAF grid).
- [[onco-sig-001-evidence]] — evidence artifact for test unit ONCO-SIG-001 (SBS-96 single-base-substitution trinucleotide context catalog — pyrimidine-strand folding; twenty-ninth Oncology unit): COSMIC SBS96 (rank 5/2, six subtypes C>A/C>G/C>T/T>A/T>C/T>G, 96 = 6×4×4, named by the pyrimidine of the mutated Watson–Crick pair) + SigProfilerMatrixGenerator Bergstrom 2019 PMC6717374 (rank 1/3, verbatim reverse-complement fold "using the purine base ... will require taking the reverse complement", mutated base centred) + Alexandrov 2013 Nature 500:415 (rank 1, 96 types, 4,938,362 mutations/7,042 cancers) + Wikipedia complementarity (rank 4, A↔T/C↔G map) sources; seven `5′,ref,alt,3′`→channel oracles (A,C,A,A→A[C>A]A no-fold · T,G,T,A→T[C>A]A fold TGA→TCA/G>T→C>A · plus three pyrimidine self-classify + three more purine folds), catalog partition invariant (exactly 96 keys, Σ counts = classifiable SBS variants); corner cases purine-ref-must-fold · non-SBS(indel/DBS) excluded · non-ACGT context unclassifiable · ref==alt out-of-scope; one cosmetic label-format assumption (`5'[REF>ALT]3'` bracket vs underline — same partition); no contradictions. This unit is catalog/classification only — NMF/NNLS exposure fitting is separate. Own concept [[sbs96-mutational-signature-catalog]].
- [[onco-sig-002-evidence]] — evidence artifact for test unit ONCO-SIG-002 (mutational signature fitting/refitting + de-novo NMF extraction; thirtieth Oncology unit, the downstream partner of ONCO-SIG-001): MutationalPatterns Blokzijl 2018 + deconstructSigs Rosenthal 2016 (rank 3, supervised **NNLS refit** `min_x ‖S·x−d‖₂², x≥0`, reconstruction `S·x`, cosine-≥0.95 gate, weights→proportions) + Lawson-Hanson 1974 (rank 4, active-set NNLS) + iMutSig Pan 2020 (rank 3, cosine) + Lee & Seung 2001 (rank 1, **NMF** multiplicative updates, Frobenius Thm 1 + KL/Poisson Thm 2, monotone non-increase, fixed point at V=WH) + Alexandrov 2013/2020 & COSMIC (rank 1–2, blind-source-separation W=signatures/H=exposures, L1-normalized 96-channel signatures) + Brunet 2004 (rank 1, consensus/**cophenetic** rank selection) + SigProfilerExtractor Islam 2022 + Rousseeuw 1987 (silhouette stability >0.80, cosine reference matching); oracles cosine (identical→1, orthogonal→0, [1,1]/[1,0]→1/√2, [3,4]/[6,8]→1) + NNLS (identity d=[3,5]→[3,5]; clamp-and-refit S=[[1,1],[0,1]], d=[0,1]→[0,0.5]; zero→[0,0]; proportions [3,5]→[0.375,0.625]) + planted-truth NMF (V=W₀H₀ residual≈0, recovered up to permutation/scaling, columns L1-sum 1) + auto-rank picks k₀=2 + cophenetic=1 at rank 1; corner cases zero catalog→zero exposures, cosine zero-norm→0.0, NMF non-convex→local-minimum (planted+fixed-seed only), permutation/scale ambiguity, ε-guarded denominators; five assumptions (Frobenius objective, seeded init, exposure proportions, zero-vector cosine 0.0, consensus-clustering/silhouette/greedy-cosine matching), no contradictions. Own concept [[mutational-signature-fitting-and-extraction]] (`depends_on` the catalog [[sbs96-mutational-signature-catalog]]).
- [[onco-sig-003-evidence]] — evidence artifact for test unit ONCO-SIG-003 (signature exposure bootstrap confidence intervals; thirty-first Oncology unit, the uncertainty layer over ONCO-SIG-002): Senkin 2021 MSA *BMC Bioinformatics* 22:540 (rank 1, parametric bootstrap, NNLS refit per replicate, 95% CI = [2.5%,97.5%] percentiles, 1000 replicates; Poisson variant = each channel independent Poisson(observedₖ), N unfixed, Poisson↔multinomial conditional equivalence) + sigminer `sig_fit_bootstrap` (rank 3, `sample(...,replace=TRUE,prob=catalog/Σ)` = fixed-N multinomial(N,p), ≥100 replicates, multinomial-only) + Huang/Wojtowicz/Przytycka 2018 *Bioinformatics* 34(2):330 (rank 1, primary bootstrap-confidence method) + Efron 1979 (rank 1, percentile CI) + Hyndman & Fan 1996 (rank 4, type-7 quantile `h=p·(n−1)`); oracles type-7 [0,1,2,3,4]→0.1/2.0/3.9 & [2,4,6,8]→2.15/5.0/7.85, single-channel [10]/[[1.0]] multinomial collapse→10/10/10/10, Poisson [12]→independent Poisson(12) positive-width, zero catalog→[0,0]; corner cases N=0 collapse, multinomial single-channel deterministic vs Poisson(λ>0) var=mean positive width, R=1→lower=upper=mean; two assumptions (type-7 interpolation, fixed seed 42), multinomial the backward-compatible default; no contradictions. Own concept [[signature-exposure-bootstrap-confidence-intervals]] (`depends_on` the fitting [[mutational-signature-fitting-and-extraction]]).
- [[onco-sig-004-evidence]] — evidence artifact for test unit ONCO-SIG-004 (mutational process classification; thirty-second Oncology unit, the aetiology-annotation layer over ONCO-SIG-002): deconstructSigs Rosenthal 2016 (rank 1/3, normalized relative contributions `Wᵢ = exposureᵢ/Σexposure` "weights between 0 and 1"; **6% presence cutoff** verbatim `signature.cutoff = 0.06` / `weights[weights < signature.cutoff] <- 0`, strict `<` so exactly 0.06 retained, empirical 1.4% false-negative rate) + COSMIC SBS proposed-aetiology strings (rank 5, label→process map SBS1/5→Aging, SBS2/13→APOBEC, SBS4→Tobacco, SBS7a–d→UV, SBS6/15/20/26→MMR deficiency) + Alexandrov 2020 *Nature* 578:94 (rank 1, the 81-signature catalogue behind COSMIC); pipeline normalize→cutoff→map→**sum per process**→active-set + `argmax` dominant; hand-derived oracle SBS2/13/1/4 = 50/30/15/5 → APOBEC 0.80 (dominant) / Aging 0.15 / Tobacco 0 (SBS4 0.05 below cutoff); corner cases surviving mass < 1 (rest unknown), multiple simultaneous processes, unmapped/"Unknown"-aetiology label → no process, Σ=0 → none; two assumptions (per-process summation, per-signature-cutoff-then-group); no contradictions. Rep. (5% tumor WES LoD, sub-percent normal band) sources; classify Somatic/Germline/NotDetected by three thresholds (f_t≥0.05 LoD, f_n≤0.01 normal-absent ceiling `normalVafThreshold`, f_n>0.01 → germline), somatic score `max(0,f_t−f_n)`, tumor-only mode; oracles A 0.25/0.00→Somatic · B 0.48/0.50→Germline · C 0.02→NotDetected · D 0.30/0.03→Germline · E tumor-only 0.20→Somatic · F/G boundaries; two source-consistent assumptions (1% normal ceiling parameterized, score a documented simplification not a caller LOD); no contradictions. Own concept [[chromothripsis-inference]] (consumes the per-segment CN states of [[copy-number-alteration-classification]]).

- [[onco-vaf-001-evidence]] — evidence artifact for test unit ONCO-VAF-001 (Variant Allele Frequency Analysis — empirical VAF + Wilson binomial CI + purity/ploidy correction; thirty-sixth Oncology unit): GATK Mutect2 FAQ (rank 3, empirical VAF = altReads/totalReads = alt AD / sum AD, distinct from the model-estimate `AF` FORMAT field) + Wikipedia Binomial-proportion-CI / Wilson 1927 JASA 22(158):209–212 (rank 4/1, Wilson score interval `center=(p̂+z²/2n)/(1+z²/n)` / `margin=(z/(1+z²/n))·√(p̂(1−p̂)/n+z²/4n²)`, z=1.96 for 95%, no-overshoot/non-zero-width vs criticised Wald) + Tarabichi 2017/2021 PMC5538405 (rank 1, diploid het clonal expected VAF = purity×0.5) + CNAqc Househam/Caravagna *Genome Biology* 2024 25:38 (rank 1, expected VAF `v=mπ/(2(1−π)+π·n_tot)`, 33%/66% 2:1 peaks, inversion `m·CCF = VAF·(2(1−π)+π·n_tot)/π` = `AdjustVAFForPurity`) sources; oracles empirical 25/100→0.25 · 0/10→0.00 · 10/10→1.00, Wilson (25,100)→0.2592 [0.1755,0.3430] & (0,10)→[0.0000,0.2775] / (10,10)→[0.7225,1.0000], correction (0.40,0.80,2)→1.00 / (0.20,0.50,2)→0.80 / (0.30,0.50,4)→1.80; corner cases VAF>1 alignment-artifact→invalid, totalReads=0→0/0 guarded, purity π=0→undefined; two source-backed assumptions (z=1.96 verbatim not 1.959964, `AdjustVAFForPurity` normal CN=2 diploid background); no contradictions. Own concept [[variant-allele-frequency-and-binomial-ci]] (the foundational VAF primitive; empirical VAF shared with [[somatic-variant-calling-tumor-normal]] / [[ctdna-detection-and-tumor-fraction]], CNAqc inversion shared with [[tumor-purity-from-mutation-vaf]] / [[cancer-cell-fraction-clonal-clustering]]).

Cross-links family anchor [[bed-format-parsing]] (tab-delimited 1-based sibling; coordinate contrast lives there — no separate concept).
- [[quality-phred-001-evidence]] — evidence artifact for test unit QUALITY-PHRED-001 (Phred score handling — parse/encode a FASTQ quality string + convert Phred+33 ↔ Phred+64; QUALITY family): **Cock et al. 2010** *Nucleic Acids Research* 38(6):1767 (DOI 10.1093/nar/gkp1137, PMC2847217) — the de-facto FASTQ spec: Phred `Q=−10·log₁₀(P)`, Sanger/**Phred+33** ASCII 33–126→Q0–93 (`Q=ord−33`), Illumina 1.3+/**Phred+64** ASCII 64–126→Q0–62, Phred score **invariant** across variants so cross-variant conversion is a pure ±31 re-offset (Solexa odds-ratio score out of scope, lossy); representability rules **Phred+64→Phred+33 always safe** (Q0–62 ⊆ 0–93) vs **Phred+33→Phred+64 overflows** for Q>62; oracles `!`/`5`/`?`/`I`/`~`→0/20/30/40/93, `@h~`→0/40/62, conversion `@h~`→`!I_` and `!I`→`@h`; must-test both-variant decode / round-trip identity / both-direction convert / out-of-range decode throws / Q>62 overflow throws / empty+null; two API-shape assumptions (malformed byte + overflow → `ArgumentOutOfRangeException`, range bounds source-backed); no contradictions. **No new concept** — enriches shared [[phred-quality-encoding]] (adds the Cock et al. primary anchor + conversion representability rules) alongside sibling [[parse-fastq-001-evidence]].
- [[quality-stats-001-evidence]] — evidence artifact for test unit QUALITY-STATS-001 (FASTQ quality statistics — Q20/Q30 fractions, mean, median, min/max, population variance/std dev; QUALITY family, sibling of QUALITY-PHRED-001): Illumina *Sequencing Quality Scores* (`% ≥ Q30` the standard NGS benchmark, **inclusive `≥`** thresholds) + Newcastle Univ. ASK (population variance/σ `= (1/N)Σ(xᵢ−μ)²`, **÷N not N−1** — quality string is the complete population) + Math is Fun (median middle element; **even count averages the two central order statistics**) + Wikipedia/Ewing & Green 1998 (Phred `Q=−10log₁₀P` provenance) + Cock et al. 2010 (Phred+33 `ord−33` decode, **cited only** — the decode is QUALITY-PHRED-001's contract, not re-tested); statistics computed over **decoded scores** so **encoding-independent** (Phred+64 same-scores → identical stats); mean = arithmetic mean of scores (a mean over log-scaled values, **not** an error-probability-averaged quality); `CalculateQ30Percentage` == `CalculateStatistics(...).PercentAboveQ30`; oracles `5?I`→20/30/40 mean 30.0 median 30 min/max 20/40 var 200/3≈66.6667 σ≈8.16497 %≥Q20 100.0 %≥Q30≈66.667, even `5II?`→median (30+40)/2=35.0 mean 32.5, single `I`(Q40)→mean=median=min=max=40 σ=0 %≥Q20/Q30 100.0; corner cases even/odd median branch, single-element σ=0, empty/null → zeroed `QualityStatistics` (TotalBases=0); one API-shape assumption (empty→zeroed not throw); no contradictions. Own concept [[fastq-quality-statistics]] (**depends on** [[phred-quality-encoding]]).
- [[rep-str-001-evidence]] — evidence artifact for test unit REP-STR-001 (Microsatellite / Short Tandem Repeat (STR) detection — perfect default `FindMicrosatellites` **plus** the opt-in approximate/imperfect/interrupted `FindApproximateTandemRepeats` + `ComputeBernoulliStatistics`, Benson **Tandem Repeats Finder** 1999 model): Benson 1999 *Nucleic Acids Research* 27(2):573 (approximate-repeat definition, seven TRF statistics, wraparound-DP alignment, majority-rule consensus) + TRF definitions/desc pages (Bernoulli adjacent-copy model, PM matching / PI indel probability, defaults PM .80/PI .10) + TRF reference impl (recommended weights `(+2,−7,−7)`, Minscore 50) + Wikipedia Microsatellite (1–6 bp unit, 5–50 copies) sources; the opt-in approximate detector **closes the exact-copies-only gap** — reports an interrupted tract as ONE repeat with percent-matches/percent-indels/score while the perfect detector fragments it; oracles `CAGCAGCAGTAGCAGCAG`→period 3 `CAG`×6 17match/1mismatch score 27 94.4%, single-base-deletion 29-bp→score 51 clears default gate, Bernoulli adjacent PM 13/15 distinct from consensus 17/18, `CACACATACACA`→PM 0.80 on-threshold; three assumptions (deterministic exhaustive (start,period) scan vs TRF probabilistic k-tuple seeding — the genome-scale residual; percentage denominator = total alignment columns; adjacent-copy segmentation for Bernoulli PM/PI, exact for substitution-only); no contradictions. **No new concept** — enriches the repeats family anchor [[repetitive-element-detection]] (Approximate STR detection section).
- [[restr-filter-001-evidence]] — evidence artifact for test unit RESTR-FILTER-001 (Restriction Enzyme Filtering — the first RESTR-* / MolTools reagent-selection unit): filter the enzyme library by end type (`GetBluntCutters()` / `GetStickyCutters()`) and by recognition-site length (`GetEnzymesByCutLength(min, max)` + single-length overload). Sources: Wikipedia *Sticky and blunt ends* (blunt = both strands terminate in a base pair, sticky = 5'/3' overhang, **blunt & sticky are the only two categories → total, disjoint partition**, blunt-blunt always compatible) + Wikipedia *Restriction enzyme* (Type II undivided palindromes **4–8 nt**; center cut→blunt / staggered→sticky; EcoRI `G^AATTC` / SmaI `CCC^GGG` / KpnI `GGTAC^C` / PstI `CTGCA^G` examples) + Wikipedia *List of restriction enzyme cutting sites* (4/6/8-bp categories) + NEB/REBASE (KpnI 3' overhang, EcoRI 5' overhang) + PMC/REBASE (SfiI interrupted palindrome `GGCCNNNN^NGGCC`, 13 nt, outside 4–8). Dataset oracle: SmaI/EcoRV/AluI/HaeIII blunt vs EcoRI(5')/KpnI(3')/PstI(3')/NotI/TaqI sticky + SfiI 13-nt interrupted. Contract: blunt ∪ sticky = full library & disjoint; `[min,max]` **inclusive** (`6→6` all 6-cutters, `9→10` none, `[4,8]` whole undivided library **except** 13-nt SfiI); single-length overload agrees at `min==max`; `min>max`/negative/zero → empty. One API-shape assumption (inclusive range bounds; recognition-length values source-backed). No contradictions. New concept [[restriction-enzyme-filtering]].
- [[rna-dotbracket-001-evidence]] — evidence artifact for test unit RNA-DOTBRACKET-001 (Dot-Bracket / extended WUSS notation — **parse & validate** a structure string; the notation/representation layer of the RNA secondary-structure family): `RnaSecondaryStructure.ParseDotBracket` (structure string → base pairs) + `ValidateDotBracket` (well-formedness). Sources: ViennaRNA *RNA Structure Notations* / *Dot-Bracket Notation* (rank 3 — base pairs = matching `()`, unpaired = `.`; extended notation adds `<>`/`{}`/`[]` + uppercase/lowercase letter pairs; **families are not required to nest → pseudoknots**; uppercase = 5' opener / lowercase = 3' closer) + ViennaRNA WUSS / `vrna_db_from_WUSS()` + Infernal Nawrocki & Eddy 2013 (rank 3 — **any matched pair = a base pair, symbol has no meaning if partners match**; flatten treats letter-pair pseudoknots as unpaired → each family an **independent pairing system**) + Rfam glossary (rank 5 — `<>`/`()`/`[]`/`{}` all pair; non-bracket `-`/`,`/`:`/`.` all single-stranded). Algorithm: **one balanced-bracket stack per family** (shared stack would mis-pair `([)]`); a closer must match a same-family opener. Oracles — parse `((((....))))`→(0,11),(1,10),(2,9),(3,8), `([)]`→`(`:(0,2)+`[`:(1,3), `<<<<[[[[....>>>>]]]]` / `((((AAAA....))))aaaa`→two 4-bp crossing helices; validate `(((...)))`/`(([[]]))`/`([)]`→**true**, `(((...)` / `...)` / `)(` / `(]`→**false**. Two API-contract assumptions (malformed input → best-effort parse dropping unmatched closers, gate with `ValidateDotBracket`; empty/null → valid pair-free). No contradictions. New concept [[rna-dot-bracket-notation]].
- [[rna-energy-001-evidence]] — evidence artifact for test unit RNA-ENERGY-001 (**Free Energy Calculation**; the thermodynamic/energy layer of the RNA secondary-structure family): `RnaSecondaryStructure.CalculateStackingEnergy`/`CalculateStemEnergy`/`CalculateHairpinLoopEnergy`/`CalculateMinimumFreeEnergy`, the **Turner 2004 nearest-neighbor** free-energy terms summed into a fold's ΔG° at 37 °C. Sources: **NNDB (Nearest Neighbor Database) Turner04** (definitive parameter tables — WC/GU stacking, hairpin `loop.txt`, terminal-mismatch, tri/tetra/hexaloop totals, hairpin bonuses/penalties) + Turner 2004 + Mathews 2004 (PNAS 101:7287) + Xia 1998 + SantaLucia 1998 + Heus & Pardi 1991; reference impls ViennaRNA / MFOLD / RNAstructure. Model `ΔG°total = init + Σstacking + Σloops`. Key parameters — WC stacking **all negative** (GC-rich most stable, `GC/CG` −3.42, `GG/CC` −3.26; `AA/UU` −0.93); **G-U wobble variable, two positive** (`UG/GU` +0.30, `GU/UG` +1.29), note-a `GG/UU`=−0.5, note-b `5'GGUC/3'CUGG` special 3-stack total −4.12 (vs −1.77); **hairpin-loop init positive & non-monotonic** (3→5.4, 4→5.6, 6→5.4, 9→6.4, Jacobson-Stockmayer beyond 9); special UNCG/GNRA tri/tetra/hexaloop total energies; all-C loop penalty (3-nt +1.5 / >3-nt 0.3n+1.6); terminal mismatch (96); +0.45 per AU/GU end. Oracles GC 3-bp stem −5.78, NNDB hairpin example-1 `GGGAUAAAUCCC` −3.42, GGUC/CUGG −4.12; single base pair / empty / poly-A → **ΔG°=0** (stacking needs ≥2 adjacent pairs). No assumptions remain (all params = exact NNDB match); three **defined conditions** (37 °C, 2-dp precision, unknown stacks→0.0). No contradictions. New concept [[rna-free-energy-turner-model]].
- [[rna-hairpin-001-evidence]] — evidence artifact for test unit RNA-HAIRPIN-001 (**Hairpin Loop and Stem Free-Energy Calculation**, Turner 2004 NN model): a focused deep-dive on `RnaSecondaryStructure.CalculateHairpinLoopEnergy` + `CalculateStemEnergy`, **not** a stem-loop enumerator and **not** miRNA-specific — it enriches the energy-layer concept [[rna-free-energy-turner-model]] (sibling of [[rna-energy-001-evidence]]) rather than defining a new one; distinct from the miRNA hairpin *finder* [[pre-mirna-hairpin-detection]]. Source: **NNDB Turner 2004** hairpin pages (via Wayback) + **Mathews et al. 2004** PNAS 101:7287. Hairpin ΔG° = init(n) + terminal mismatch + first-mismatch bonuses (UU/GA −0.9, GG −0.8) + special-GU-closure −2.2 (**G-U only, not U-G** — documented asymmetry) + all-C penalty (3-nt +1.5, >3-nt 0.3n+1.6); **3-nt loops get no first-mismatch term**; loops < 3 nt prohibited; special tri/tetra/hexaloop totals override the model (`CAACG` 6.8, `CCUCGG` 2.5). Stem = per-stack stacking + **+0.45/AU-end**, P pairs → **P−1 stacks** (P ≤ 1 ⇒ 0). Oracles NNDB Example 1 (A-U closing, 6-nt loop A…A) loop +4.6 + helix −6.01 = **−1.4**; Example 2 (5-nt loop G…G, GG bonus) loop +4.1 + helix −6.01 = **−1.9**; all-C 3-nt loop 6.9, 4-nt 7.7. One display-precision item (2-dp intermediate rounding, tests assert `.Within(1e-9)`); no contradictions. **No new concept** — enriches [[rna-free-energy-turner-model]].
- [[rna-invert-001-evidence]] — evidence artifact for test unit RNA-INVERT-001 (RNA inverted repeats / potential stem regions — antiparallel **reverse-complement arms** that form a stem-loop; RNA secondary-structure family, `RnaSecondaryStructure`): IUPACpal (Alamro 2021, PMC7866733) `W G W̄ᴿ` gapped model + *k*-Hamming mismatch (perfect = k=0) + Watson-Crick RNA complement (A⟷U, C⟷G) + Wikipedia/Ussery 2008 (`5'---TTACGnnnnnnCGTAA---3'`, zero-gap ⇒ palindrome) + EMBOSS `einverted` (inverted repeat = stem-loop = local alignment of a sequence vs its reverse complement) sources; oracles `UUACGAAAAAACGUAA` (arm `UUACG` 0–4 / loop 5–10 / arm `CGUAA` 11–15) and palindromic `GGCCAAAGGCC` (left 0–3 / right 7–10 / len 4); MUST antiparallel-not-parallel + no-IR→empty; scope restriction = **perfect ungapped `k=0`** arms only (einverted scored mismatch/gap DP Not Implemented), loop bounds via minSpacing/maxSpacing, maximal-arm non-overlapping greedy reporting; no contradictions. **No new concept** — reuses [[repetitive-element-detection]] (same IUPACpal IR model) + [[rna-base-pairing]] (antiparallel RNA complement) + [[pre-mirna-hairpin-detection]]/[[rna-dot-bracket-notation]] (stem-loop framing).
- [[rna-mfe-001-evidence]] — evidence artifact for test unit RNA-MFE-001 (**Minimum Free Energy (MFE) RNA secondary-structure prediction** — the Zuker–Stiegler dynamic-programming folder; the folding/search layer of the RNA secondary-structure family, `RnaSecondaryStructure.CalculateMinimumFreeEnergy` / `PredictStructure`). Sources: **Zuker & Stiegler 1981** *NAR* 9(1):133 (rank 1 — original MFE DP, loop decomposition hairpin/stacking/bulge-interior/multibranch, polynomial) + **Lorenz 2011** ViennaRNA 2.0 (rank 3 — MFE fold "derived from the Zuker–Stiegler decomposition", **O(n³)**) + **Ward 2017** *NAR* 45(14):8541 (rank 1 — C(i,j)=min(hairpin, interior/bulge, multiloop) + multiloop M/M1 + exterior F matrices, **standard affine multiloop → O(n³) time / O(n²) space**, "simplest model is best") + **NNDB Turner 2004** worked examples + **Mathews 2004** PNAS 101:7287. The unit that **consumes** the [[rna-free-energy-turner-model]] Turner terms and **produces** a [[rna-dot-bracket-notation]] structure. Oracles `CalculateMinimumFreeEnergy("CACAAAAAAAUGUG")`=−1.41 (NNDB Example 1, structure `((((......))))`), `CACAGAAAGUGUG`=−1.91 (Example 2, GG first mismatch). Invariants INV-01 MFE ≤ 0, INV-02 suffix-monotone `MFE(s) ≤ MFE(prefix)`, INV-03 optimized DP == classic O(n³) baseline; empty/null / homopolymer `AAAAAAAA` / sequence `< minLoopSize+2` (`GCGC`) → 0 (min hairpin loop 3 nt); intramolecular ⇒ no helix-init constant. Two documented simplifications (multiloop per-unpaired `c=0` with `a=9.25`/helix `c=−0.63`; 2-dp rounding, tests `.Within(1e-9)` + `Round(mfe,1)`==NNDB), no source contradictions. **New concept** [[rna-minimum-free-energy-folding]]; the folder the [[pre-mirna-hairpin-detection]] `AssessHairpinByMfe` path (prior pages' generic *RNA-STRUCT-001*) uses.
- [[rna-pair-001-evidence]] — evidence artifact for test unit RNA-PAIR-001 (**RNA Base Pairing** — the RNA-secondary-structure family's own base-pairing primitive): `RnaSecondaryStructure.CanPair` / `GetBasePairType` (typed `WatsonCrick`/`Wobble`/`null` classifier) / `GetComplement`. Sources: **Crick 1966** *J Mol Biol* 19:548 (wobble hypothesis — G pairs C(WC)+U(wobble), U pairs A(WC)+G(wobble); G-U the only standard wobble, distinct from WC) + Wikipedia *Base pair* (canonical A•U 2 H-bonds / G•C 3 H-bonds, pairing reciprocal) + Wikipedia *Wobble base pair* + IUPAC-IUB 1970 *Biochemistry* 9(20):4022 (complement table) + Biopython `complement_rna("CGAUT")`→`"GCUAA"`. Rule {A-U, U-A, G-C, C-G}=WatsonCrick, {G-U, U-G}=Wobble, all else false/null; complement A→U/U→A/G→C/C→G/**T→A**(DNA T=U)/N→N/R→Y; symmetry `f(x,y)==f(y,x)`; non-alphabet→false/null no exception. One non-correctness normalization (case-insensitive upper-casing). No contradictions. **No new concept** — enriches the shared [[rna-base-pairing]] primitive (the MIRNA-PAIR-001 sibling), adding the typed `GetBasePairType` classifier surface.
- [[rna-partition-001-evidence]] — evidence artifact for test unit RNA-PARTITION-001 (**RNA partition function (McCaskill) and Boltzmann structure probability** — the probabilistic/ensemble layer of the RNA secondary-structure family): the Boltzmann-weighted counterpart of MFE folding that computes the equilibrium partition function `Z`, per-base-pair binding probabilities, and the Boltzmann probability of a given structure. Sources: **McCaskill 1990** *Biopolymers* 29(6-7):1105 (rank 1, PMID 1695107 — full equilibrium partition function + substructure probabilities, **O(n³) recursion**) + **S. Will MIT 18.417 (2011)** slides (rank 1 — inside `Q_ij = Q_{i,j-1} + Σ_k Q_{i,k-1}·Q^b_{kj}`, `Z = Q_{1n}`, base case `Q_ij=1` for i≥j−m; outside base-pair-probability recursion; `Pr[P|S]=Z⁻¹exp(−βE(P))`) + **Freiburg McCaskill tool** (rank 3 — simplified fixed-per-pair `E_bp` model, WC+GU pairing) + **ViennaRNA pf_fold** (rank 3 — `p(s)=e^(−βE(s))/Z`, default 37 °C = 310.15 K, RT = 0.61626805). **Correction (2026-06-16):** base-pair probability requires the **outside** recursion `p_kl = Q^b_kl·O_kl/Z`; the external-only term is **wrong for nestable pairs** (`GGGAAACCC` P(2,6)=6/20 not external 1/20; verified to 3.3e-16 vs Boltzmann brute force). Oracles (E_bp=0 ⇒ Z counts structures): `AAAA`→1, `GC`→1, `GGGGCCCC`→16, `GGGAAACCC`→20 (two independent derivations). Invariants Z ≥ 1 (empty structure weight 1), P(i,j) ∈ [0,1] + symmetric, per-base pairing sum ≤ 1 (300 random seqs, max 0.983), monotone in E_bp; min-loop m forbids j−k ≤ m pairs, WC+GU only. One simplification (fixed-per-pair `E_bp` energy model vs full Turner NN — energy model only; recurrence + probabilities + invariants conformant with McCaskill 1990), no source contradictions. **New concept** [[rna-partition-function-mccaskill]] — the ensemble/`alternative_to` counterpart of [[rna-minimum-free-energy-folding]].
- [[rna-pkpredict-001-evidence]] — evidence artifact for test unit RNA-PKPREDICT-001 (**Pseudoknot structure prediction — canonical H-type, pknotsRG class**; the **crossing-helix layer** of the RNA secondary-structure family, `RnaSecondaryStructure`): predict the optimal fold that may contain a single simple recursive pseudoknot (two **crossing** helices, `i<k<j<l` Antczak 2018) — the one feature the nested [[rna-minimum-free-energy-folding|MFE]] / [[rna-partition-function-mccaskill|McCaskill]] predictors cannot represent. Sources: **Reeder & Giegerich 2004** *BMC Bioinformatics* 5:104 (rank 1, PMC514697 — pknotsRG "two crossing helices with three intervening loops", grammar `a~~~u~~~b~~~v~~~a'~~~w~~~b'`, **O(n⁴)/O(n²)**, canonization rules, penalties) + **pknotsRG `Energy.lhs`** source (rank 3 — verbatim penalties + same-NN-model helices, no extra per-pair penalty) + **Wikipedia/Rivas & Eddy 1999** (H-type 5'→3' stem1-5'→loop1→stem2-5'→loop2→stem1-3'→loop3→stem2-3', two-layer `()`/`[]`) + **PDB 437D / Su 1999** (BWYV real H-type, tertiary-stabilized) + **Antczak 2018** (crossing `i<k<j<l`). Energy = Turner NN stacking both helices + penalties **pseudoknot initiation 9.0** (anti-spurious-knot gate) / **unpaired loop nt 0.3** / **base pair inside knot 0.0** (kcal/mol). Canonization: equal-length bulge-free helices / maximal extent / fixed overlap boundary. Oracles designed H-type `GGGGAACCCCAACCCCAAGGGG`→`HasPseudoknot==true`, stems (0,15)…(3,12)+(6,21)…(9,18), two-layer `((((..[[[[..))))..]]]]`, ΔG<MFE; plain hairpin `GGGGAAAACCCC`→`HasPseudoknot==false` = MFE `((((....))))`; BWYV `GGCGCGGCACCGUCCGCGGAACAAACGG`→NN optimum is the stem-1 hairpin **not** the knot (documented NN-only limit). Invariants `FreeEnergy ≤ CalculateMfeStructure().FreeEnergy` (MFE fallback), no spurious knot, each position paired ≤1× + ≥1 genuine crossing; empty/null/too-short→empty pair-free ΔG 0. One documented scope note (PARTIAL pknotsRG coverage — single canonical H-type only; recursively-nested / over-arching / multiple knots **not** implemented; loops fold with the existing MFE). No contradictions. **New concept** [[rna-pseudoknot-prediction]] — the crossing-structure complement of the nested MFE folder + McCaskill ensemble.
- [[rna-pkrecursive-001-evidence]] — evidence artifact for test unit RNA-PKRECURSIVE-001 (**Recursive pknotsRG pseudoknot prediction — nested / multiple / over-arching H-type knots**; the **recursive-grammar extension** of the single-knot RNA-PKPREDICT-001, `RnaSecondaryStructure`): predict the optimal fold that may contain **several** pseudoknots and knots **nested inside loops / over-arched by an enclosing helix**, filling exactly the PARTIAL-coverage gap the single-knot unit recorded. **Same pknotsRG class** (Reeder & Giegerich 2004/2007) — same Turner-NN energy on both helices, same penalties **initiation 9.0 / unpaired loop nt 0.3 / pair inside knot 0.0** kcal/mol, same canonization rules — but the three loops *u*/*v*/*w* now fold by the **same recursive folder** (a loop may contain a further knot), the top level **chains multiple knots**, and an enclosing helix may **over-arch** a knot. Sources: **Reeder & Giegerich 2004** *BMC Bioinformatics* 5:104 (loops "fold internally … **including simple recursive pseudoknots**", **O(n⁴)/O(n²)**, canonization 8→4 boundaries vs Rivas & Eddy O(n⁶)/O(n⁴)) + **Reeder, Steffen & Giegerich 2007** *NAR* 35:W320 (per-interval **competition** with unknotted foldings — the whole-sequence mechanism enabling multiple/nested knots) + **pknotsRG `Energy.lhs`** (verbatim 9.0/0.3/0.0) + **Antczak 2018** (crossing `i<k<j<l`). Constructed fully-derivable oracles: over-arching `AAAAAAAAGGGGAACCCCAACCCCAAGGGGUUUUUUUU` (38 nt)→`((((((((((((..[[[[..))))..]]]]))))))))` **ΔG −14.37** (single-knot/MFE both −13.05, no combined structure); two-knot 80-nt→**two** crossing knots (crossing-count 32) **ΔG −28.74** (single/MFE −27.14, none); plain `GGGGAAAACCCC`→ no knot = MFE; single-knot parity `GGGGAACCCCAACCCCAAGGGG`→identical −8.76. Invariants recursive ΔG ≤ MFE (0 violations, 150-seq random sweep), no spurious knots, each position paired ≤1× + ≥1 crossing; empty/null/too-short→empty pair-free. **Excluded** (verbatim): triple-crossing helices, kissing hairpins, bulged/unequal-length helices. Two scope notes: PARTIAL recursion (realizes the recursive *class* via maximal-extent helix scan, not bit-identical to the reference 4-boundary ADP parser) + two-simultaneous-knot cases are **engineered** (isolated A·U clamps — two strong G·C knots are the genuine MFE only when the cross-region nested alternative is suppressed). No contradictions. **Enriches** [[rna-pseudoknot-prediction]] (§6, the recursive extension of the single-knot concept — no new concept).
- [[rna-pseudoknot-001-evidence]] — evidence artifact for test unit RNA-PSEUDOKNOT-001 (**Pseudoknot detection** — identify **crossing** base pairs in a **given** structure; the detection/analysis facet of the RNA crossing-helix family, `RnaSecondaryStructure.DetectPseudoknots`): given a base-pair **set** (not a sequence), a pure **O(n²) combinatorial scan** reports every crossing pair-of-pairs `i<k<j<l`. Sources: **Antczak et al. 2018** *Bioinformatics* 34(8):1304 (rank 1 — crossing/conflict `i<j<i'<j'`, pseudoknot **order** = min base-pair-set decompositions to nested, DBL notation order 0 `()`/1 `[]`/2 `{}`/3 `<>`/4–8 letters, H-type `([)]`) + **Smit, Rother, Heringa & Knight 2008** *RNA* 14(3):410 (rank 1 — pseudoknot presence *requires* crossing pairs; order-assignment / pseudoknot-removal family) + **biotite.structure.pseudoknots** (rank 3 — crossing = not purely nestable; nested order 0 / knotted order 1+) + **Wikipedia Pseudoknot** (rank 4, cites Rivas & Eddy 1999). Crossing `i<k<j<l` = pseudoknot; two exhaustive negatives **nested** `i<k<l<j` + **disjoint** `j<k`. Oracles `([)]`=(0,2)+(1,3)→`0<1<2<3`→one pseudoknot, nested (0,5)+(1,4)→none, disjoint (0,2)+(3,5)→none. Invariants ≥2 pairs required / endpoints normalized min-max to open<close / deterministic / every reported knot satisfies `i<k<j<l`. **Distinct** from the energy-driven [[rna-pseudoknot-prediction]] predictor (pair set vs sequence, O(n²) scan vs O(n⁴) energy DP) — it *is* the crossing primitive that predictor's validity invariant leans on. One scope note: pseudoknot-**order** grouping (DBL layering) Not Implemented (reports the binary crossing relations); no contradictions. **New concept** [[rna-pseudoknot-detection]] — the analysis-side sibling of the crossing-helix predictor.
- [[rna-stemloop-001-evidence]] — evidence artifact for test unit RNA-STEMLOOP-001 (**Stem-Loop (Hairpin) Detection**, area `RnaStructure`): the **enumeration layer** of the RNA secondary-structure family — `FindStemLoops(sequence, minStem, minLoop, maxLoop, allowWobble)` / `FindHairpins` **scan a sequence for every stem-loop** it can form (stem of antiparallel WC/wobble pairs + apical loop), an **O(n²·L)** scan distinct from the single-optimal [[rna-minimum-free-energy-folding|MFE folder]], the hairpin *energy* unit [[rna-hairpin-001-evidence]], and the miRNA-specific [[pre-mirna-hairpin-detection]]. Sources: Wikipedia (Stem-loop / Tetraloop / Pseudoknot — loop **≥3 nt** steric floor, optimal **4-8 nt**; UUCG+GNRA **~70%** of 16S-rRNA tetraloops) + Woese 1990 (PNAS 87:8467) + Antao 1991 (NAR 19:5901, **UUCG most stable**) + Heus & Pardi 1991 (Science 253:191) + Rivas & Eddy 1999 (pseudoknot alg) + NNDB Turner 2004 (tetraloop energetics). Tetraloop families **GNRA** (GAAA/GCAA/GGAA/GUAA) / **UNCG** (UACG/UCCG/UGCG/UUCG) / **CUUG**, ~3.0 kcal/mol bonus; `FindPseudoknots` flags crossing pairs `i<k<j<l` (same primitive as [[rna-pseudoknot-detection]]). Oracles `GGGAAAACCC`→`(((....)))` (3-bp stem + AAAA loop), `GGGCGAAAGCCC`→GNRA tetraloop, `AAAA…`/`GC`/`GCAUC`→none. Invariants non-overlap / ≤1 pair per base / contiguous loop / antiparallel stem; defaults wobble-on, minLoop 3, minStem 3. Limitations: no PK prediction from sequence, simplified energy, no internal loops/bulges, single structure. No contradictions. **New concept** [[rna-stem-loop-enumeration]].
- [[rna-struct-001-evidence]] — evidence artifact for test unit RNA-STRUCT-001 (**Secondary Structure Prediction**, area `RnaStructure`): the **top-level structure-prediction umbrella** on `RnaSecondaryStructure` — `Predict(sequence)` (a **Nussinov & Jacobson 1980** O(n³)/O(n²) base-pair-**maximizing** DP), `PredictWithConstraints` (forced base pairs, Mathews 2004), `ToDotBracket`/`FromDotBracket` (notation round-trip). Headline objective = maximize the **(weighted) base-pair count** (WC −2.0 / wobble −1.0), "**relative stability, not physical energy units**" — a **distinct sibling** of the physical-kcal/mol [[rna-minimum-free-energy-folding|RNA-MFE-001]], **not an alias**: both live on `RnaSecondaryStructure` and share its Zuker MFE machinery (this unit's **deviation D5** added `CalculateMfeStructure`/`PredictStructureMfe`, the Zuker–Stiegler traceback partner of RNA-MFE-001's `PredictStructure`). Stem-loop energy model uses Turner 2004 / NNDB terms ([[rna-free-energy-turner-model]]). Sources: Nussinov & Jacobson 1980 (*PNAS* 77:6309) + Zuker & Stiegler 1981 (*NAR* 9:133) + MIT 6.047 Lec 08 (Washietl 2012, explicit F/C/M/M¹ recurrences) + Turner 2004/NNDB + Mathews 2004 (*PNAS* 101:7287) + Wikipedia. Oracles simple hairpin `GGGGAAAACCCC`→`((((....))))`, GNRA `GCGCGAAACGCGC`→GA first-mismatch −0.9, tRNA-like 72-nt cloverleaf, poly-A `AAAAAAAAAAAA`→no pairs/MFE 0. Invariants dot-bracket balance / MFE sign ≤ 0 / WC stacking negative / loop init positive / non-overlap / ≤1 pair per base; empty/null→MFE 0, min hairpin 3-bp stem + 3-nt loop, case-insensitive. **Pseudoknots detected (not predicted)** via the `i<k<j<l` crossing test ([[rna-pseudoknot-detection]]); D1/D2/D5 resolved, D3 int21 (2,304) / D4 int22 (36,864) internal-loop lookup tables BLOCKED (too large for inline static data). No source contradictions; one wiki reconciliation (RNA-STRUCT-001 ≠ RNA-MFE-001, superseding the earlier alias assumption). **New concept** [[rna-secondary-structure-prediction]].
- [[phylo-boot-001-evidence]] — evidence artifact for test unit PHYLO-BOOT-001 (Phylogenetic Bootstrap Analysis — Felsenstein's bootstrap proportions; first phylogenetics PHYLO-* unit): Felsenstein 1985 *Evolution* 39(4):783 (origin — resample characters with replacement, same sample size, keep species; *P* = fraction of bootstrap samples a group appears in; 95%→significant) + Lemoine 2018 *Nature* 556:452 PMC6030568 (same-length pseudo-alignments; support = proportion of pseudo-trees containing that branch; branch = bipartition; binary per-replicate) + Biopython `Bio.Phylo.Consensus` (`bootstrap`/`bootstrap_trees`/`get_support` — column resample `randint(0,length-1)`, clades matched **by terminal leaf-name set**, only `find_clades(terminal=False)` scored, `(t+1)*100/size`) sources; oracles two-group `AAAAAAAAAA`/`AAAAAAAAAA`/`GGGGGGGGGG`/`GGGGGGGGGG` UPGMA+JukesCantor 100 reps seed 42 → support{A,B}=support{C,D}=1.0 (saturated JC distances → identical topology every replicate), all-identical `ACGTACGT`→every clade 1.0; MUST-test support∈[0,1] / determinism / keys=non-trivial reference clades / support=k/replicates, input validation null/<2-seq/replicates<1 throw; two source-consistent assumptions (rooted-clade scoring vs unrooted bipartitions matching Biopython, proportion [0,1] vs percentage ×100); no contradictions. Own concept [[phylogenetic-bootstrap-support]].
- [[phylo-comp-001-evidence]] — evidence artifact for test unit PHYLO-COMP-001 (Tree Comparison — Robinson–Foulds distance, MRCA, patristic distance; second phylogenetics PHYLO-* unit): Wikipedia Robinson–Foulds metric / MRCA / Phylogenetic tree + Robinson & Foulds 1981 (doi:10.1016/0025-5564(81)90043-2, RF proper metric via splits) + Smith 2020 (generalized RF) + Day 1985 (linear-time) sources; RF = symmetric difference `A+B` of canonical split sets (raw count, even, rooted-clade = dummy-leaf), **max RF = 2(n−2) rooted vs 2(n−3) unrooted** reconciled by dummy-leaf equivalence; MRCA O(n) recursive leaf-name traversal (not-in-tree→null), patristic = `dist(x,MRCA)+dist(y,MRCA)` (not-in-tree→NaN, zero-branches→0); invariants RF identity/symmetric/≥0/even, MRCA symmetric/always-ancestor/unique, patristic PD(x,x)=0/symmetric/≥0; two source-backed scope decisions (binary-only via `PhyloNode` Left/Right, rooted-only via UPGMA/NJ); no deviations, no contradictions. Own concept [[tree-comparison-metrics]].
- [[phylo-dist-001-evidence]] — evidence artifact for test unit PHYLO-DIST-001 (Phylogenetic Distance Matrix Calculation; third phylogenetics PHYLO-* unit): Wikipedia Models-of-DNA-evolution / Substitution-model / Distance-matrices-in-phylogeny + Jukes & Cantor 1969 + Kimura 1980 + Felsenstein 2004 sources; `CalculatePairwiseDistance`/`CalculateDistanceMatrix` over four methods **Hamming** (raw count) / **p-distance** (`differences/comparableSites`) / **JC69** (`-3/4·ln(1−4p/3)`) / **K2P** (`-1/2·ln((1−2S−V)·√(1−2V))`, S=transition/V=transversion); matrix symmetric / zero-diagonal / non-negative / *n×n*, correction ordering JC69≥p & K2P≥p, triangle-inequality expected-not-guaranteed; pairwise deletion (gaps + IUPAC N/R/Y skipped), case-insensitive; **JC69 saturates p≥3/4→+∞ / K2P V≥1/2→+∞**, all-gap/empty→0, unequal-length→ArgumentException; oracles `ACGTACGT`/`TCGTACGT`→Hamming 1/p 0.125/JC69≈0.137, transition `GCGT` K2P≈0.34657 vs transversion `CCGT`≈0.31713, mixed≈0.30679, gap→7 sites; two API-contract assumptions (empty/all-gap→0, pairwise deletion); no contradictions. Own concept [[evolutionary-distance-matrix]].

- [[phylo-tree-001-evidence]] — evidence artifact for test unit PHYLO-TREE-001 (Phylogenetic Tree Construction — UPGMA & Neighbor-Joining; the phylogenetics PHYLO-* tree-building core): Wikipedia UPGMA / Neighbor-joining / Phylogenetic-tree + Saitou & Nei 1987 (MBE 4(4):406–425, NJ) + Sokal & Michener 1958 (UPGMA) + Felsenstein 2004 sources; `BuildTree`/`BuildTreeFromMatrix` consume the distance matrix and emit a `PhyloNode` tree via two agglomerative methods — **UPGMA** (rooted ultrametric, molecular clock, **height=d/2**, arithmetic-mean update, O(n³)/O(n²)) and **NJ** (unrooted/midpoint-rooted, clock-free, **Q(i,j)=(n−2)·d(i,j)−Σd(i,k)−Σd(j,k)** join minimum-Q, δ(f,u)=d(f,g)/2+(Σd(f,k)−Σd(g,k))/(2(n−2)), additive-matrix topology guarantee, **negative branches preserved, not clamped**, O(n³)); invariants all-taxa-leaves / binary / n leaves+n−1 internal / UPGMA branches≥0 / UPGMA ultrametric+rooted / NJ additive-correct+may-be-negative+no-clock; oracles UPGMA 5S-rRNA matrix→(a,b)@17→((a,b),e)@22→(c,d)@28→final@33, δ(a,u)=8.5/δ(e,v)=11/δ(c,w)=14/root 16.5 (tips all 16.5, tol 1e-10), NJ 5-taxon→first join (a,b) **Q₁(a,b)=−50**, δ(a,u)=2/δ(b,u)=3/δ(u,v)=3/δ(c,v)=4/δ(v,w)=2/δ(d,w)=2/δ(e,w)=1 (patristic recovers input); edge cases <2/unequal→throw, identical→arbitrary join, all-equal→star, saturated p>0.75→JC +∞; 32 runs (M01–M13/S01–S05/C01–C05), S06 removed (dup of S02); deviations None (§8). Own concept [[distance-based-tree-construction]].
- [[pop-ancestry-001-evidence]] — evidence artifact for test unit POP-ANCESTRY-001 (Ancestry Estimation — supervised/projection ADMIXTURE, estimate ancestry proportions Q by EM with **fixed** reference allele frequencies F; **first population-genetics POP-\* unit**): Alexander, Novembre & Lange 2009 *Genome Research* 19(9):1655 (rank 1 — genotype g∈{0,1,2}=allele-1 count, Q I×K / F K×J, **log-likelihood Eq. 2** `L=ΣᵢΣⱼ{g·ln(Σq·f)+(2−g)·ln(Σq·(1−f))}` under `Σ_k q_ik=1`, **FRAPPE EM Eq. 4** `q^{n+1}=(1/2J)Σⱼ[g·a+(2−g)·b]`, convergence Eq. 5 ΔL<ε default 10⁻⁴, cost O(IJK²), K! label-permutation maxima) + Alexander & Lange 2011 *BMC Bioinformatics* 12:246 (supervised mode — labelled reference individuals as training samples, less allele-freq uncertainty; full text Springer-gated) + ADMIXTURE 1.4 Manual §2.10 supervised / §2.14 projection (reference rows of Q pinned, refs 100% single-ancestry; learned F as fixed input `admixture -P`) sources; oracles symmetric K=2 J=2 panel f_A=[0.8,0.2]/f_B=[0.2,0.8] g=[2,0] from (0.5,0.5) → **one EM iter (0.8,0.2) exactly** → (0.9412,0.0588) → converges (1.0,0.0), single-SNP f=[0.9,0.1] g=2→(0.9,0.1)/g=1→(0.5,0.5) uninformative-het/g=0→(0.1,0.9), identical panels uniform fixed point; MUST Σ_k q=1 / EM-ascent L non-decreasing / diagnostic→source; two assumptions (maxIterations budget augments ε=10⁻⁴ convergence — same fixed point; missing genotype ∉{0,1,2} skipped); label non-identifiability pinned by fixed labelled panels; no contradictions. Own concept [[ancestry-estimation-admixture]].
- [[pop-div-001-evidence]] — evidence artifact for test unit POP-DIV-001 (Diversity statistics — nucleotide diversity π, Watterson's θ, Tajima's D, heterozygosity; **second population-genetics POP-\* unit**, sibling of POP-ANCESTRY-001): Nei & Li 1979 *PNAS* (π = Σ_{i<j} d_ij / (C(n,2)·L), mean per-site pairwise differences) + Watterson 1975 *TPB* (θ̂_W = S/a_n, a_n = Σ_{i=1}^{n−1} 1/i harmonic number; per-site θ_W = S/(a_n·L)) + Tajima 1989 *Genetics* (D = (k̂ − S/a_1)/√(e_1·S + e_2·S(S−1)), **k̂ = average pairwise-difference COUNT not per-site π**, variance terms a_1/a_2/b_1/b_2/c_1/c_2/e_1/e_2; D≈0 neutral / D<0 excess rare alleles=sweep-or-expansion / D>0 deficit=balancing-or-contraction) + Nei 1978 *Genetics* (unbiased gene diversity H_obs = n/(n−1)·H_exp, H_exp = (1/L)Σ(1−Σp²); haploid H_obs ≡ π) sources; all "exact match" no deviations; Wikipedia oracle n=5/L=20/S=4/a_1=25/12 → k̂=2.0/π=0.1/S/a_1≈1.92/d=0.08/θ_W≈0.096 → **D≈0.273** (TD-C01/TD-C02); edge cases n=0→0, n=1→π0/θ undef, n=2→π defined but **D undefined→0** (needs n≥3), S=0/monomorphic→all 0, Var≤0→D=0; API note `CalculateTajimasD(k̂, S, n)` takes k̂ NOT per-site π; no contradictions. Own concept [[genetic-diversity-statistics]].
- [[pop-freq-001-evidence]] — evidence artifact for test unit POP-FREQ-001 (Allele & genotype frequencies — major/minor frequencies, MAF, MAF filtering; foundational population-genetics POP-\* primitive): Wikipedia *Allele frequency* / *Genotype frequency* (biallelic `p = f(AA) + ½f(AB)`, `q = f(BB) + ½f(AB)`, **`p + q = 1`**; allele-counting `total = 2·(n_AA+n_AB+n_BB)`, `major = 2·n_AA+n_AB`, `minor = 2·n_BB+n_AB`; four-o'clock oracle 49/42/9 → freq(a)=0.30/freq(A)=0.70) + Wikipedia *Minor allele frequency* (`MAF = min(alt_freq, 1−alt_freq)`, **`0 ≤ MAF ≤ 0.5`**; HapMap MAF ≥ 0.05, common>0.05 vs rare<0.05) + VCF/PLINK dosage encoding (0=hom-ref/1=het/2=hom-alt, `alt_freq = Σg/(2n)`) + Gillespie 2004 / NDSU PopGen sources; oracles AF-1…AF-6, MAF-1…MAF-6 (alt_freq 0.7 → MAF 0.3 symmetry; monomorphic → 0; 50/50 → 0.5), FLT-1…FLT-6 (MAF<0.01 / <0.05 / >0.4, empty/all/none); invariants p+q=1, major+minor=total, MAF symmetric 0…0.5; edge cases zero samples→(0,0), empty vector→MAF 0, **negative count → `ArgumentOutOfRangeException`**; scope = biallelic counting/normalization only (no HWE test, no multiallelic, no phasing/imputation); all exact-match, no deviations/contradictions. Own concept [[allele-genotype-frequencies]].
- [[pop-fst-001-evidence]] — evidence artifact for test unit POP-FST-001 (Fst fixation index + F-statistics Fis/Fit/Fst + pairwise Fst; population-genetics POP-\* differentiation unit, **consumes** per-population allele frequencies from POP-FREQ-001): Wikipedia *Fixation index* (**Wright 1965 variance-based** `Fst = σ_S²/(pBar(1−pBar))`; two-pop `pBar=(n1·p1+n2·p2)/(n1+n2)`, `σ_S²=(n1(p1−pBar)²+n2(p2−pBar)²)/(n1+n2)`; multi-locus **ratio-of-sums** `Σσ_S²/Σhet`; Fst∈[0,1], 0=panmixia/1=fixed differences; **not a metric** — fails triangle inequality) + Wikipedia *F-statistics* (heterozygosity partition `Fis=1−Hi/Hs`, `Fit=1−Hi/Ht`, `Fst=1−Hs/Ht`; **exact identity** `(1−Fit)=(1−Fis)(1−Fst)`) + Wright 1950/1965, Weir & Cockerham 1984 (θ estimator — cited as what is **deliberately NOT** implemented: no ANOVA/finite-sample bias correction), Holsinger & Weir 2009, Cavalli-Sforza 1994 sources; oracles identical→0, fixed p1=1/p2=0→**1.0 exactly** (pBar=.5,var=.25,het=.25), pop1=(.9,.8)/pop2=(.1,.2)→1/2, unequal sizes 0.006274…, components Fis=1/19/Fit=1/13/Fst=1/39, scale 1/2499 & 61/198, pairwise cells 1/99,4/21,3/25, excess-het **negative** Fis=−2/3/Fit=−2/5/Fst=4/25; ref values Cavalli-Sforza (Mbuti–PNG 0.4573, mean 0.1338) + Elhaik 2012 HapMap; edge cases denominator 0 (pBar=0/1, both-fixed-same, empty)→**return 0**, monomorphic→0; pairwise matrix symmetric, zero diagonal; 25 tests (−1 dup +4 new); no deviations/contradictions. Own concept [[population-differentiation-fst]].
- [[pop-hw-001-evidence]] — evidence artifact for test unit POP-HW-001 (Hardy-Weinberg equilibrium chi-square test; population-genetics POP-\* unit, **consumes** genotype counts from POP-FREQ-001): Wikipedia *Hardy-Weinberg principle* (Hardy 1908 / Weinberg 1908 — expected genotype freqs `f(AA)=p²`/`f(Aa)=2pq`/`f(aa)=q²`, Ford moth example, deviation causes, genotyping-error note) + Wikipedia *Chi-squared test* (Pearson goodness-of-fit `χ²=Σ(O−E)²/E`) + Emigh 1980 (chi-square comparison) + Wigginton et al. 2005 AJHG (**exact test** — cited as the out-of-scope alternative) sources; allele freq `p=(2·n_AA+n_Aa)/(2n)`/`q=1−p`, expected counts `E={p²n,2pqn,q²n}`, **df=1** (`#genotypes−#alleles=3−2`), p-value via chi-square CDF (lower-incomplete-gamma approx), default **α=0.05** critical 3.841; `TestHardyWeinberg` returns InEquilibrium/ChiSquare/PValue; oracles Ford moth (1469,138,5)→`p≈0.954`/`χ²≈0.83`→in-eq (HW-E01), perfect (25,50,25)→`χ²=0` (HW-E02), excess-het (10,80,10)→`χ²=36 ≫ 3.84`→out-of-eq (HW-E03), zero samples→InEquilibrium true/PValue 1 (HW-E04), fixed (100,0,0)→in-eq (HW-E05), all-het (0,100,0)→out-of-eq (HW-E06); edge cases **zero n→PValue 1** (no evidence against H₀), **expected-0 term skipped** (div-by-zero guard); scope = biallelic chi-square goodness-of-fit only (no exact test, no multiallelic); no deviations/contradictions. Own concept [[hardy-weinberg-equilibrium-test]].
- [[pop-ld-001-evidence]] — evidence artifact for test unit POP-LD-001 (Linkage disequilibrium — `CalculateLD` (D, D', r²) + `FindHaplotypeBlocks`; population-genetics POP-\* unit, **consumes** allele/haplotype frequencies from POP-FREQ-001): Wikipedia *Linkage disequilibrium* (`D = p_AB − p_A·p_B`; Lewontin 1964 `D' = |D|/D_max` with sign-branched `D_max` clamped [0,1]; Hill & Robertson 1968 `r² = D²/(p_A·q_A·p_B·q_B)`; **diploid-frequency result** `R_AB = r_AB` (Wright 1933) ⇒ r² computable **without phase**) + Wikipedia *Haplotype block* (Gabriel 2002 / Patil 2001 threshold blocks) sources; implementation `r²` = squared Pearson correlation of 0/1/2 genotype dosage vectors `Cov²/(Var·Var)`, `D` from diploid covariance `Cov=2D ⇒ D=Cov/2`; `FindHaplotypeBlocks` = simplified adjacent-pair Gabriel (consecutive `r² ≥ threshold`, default **0.7**, ≥2 variants); oracles perfect LD (identical vectors)→`r²≈1`, no LD (balanced)→`r²≈0`, anti-correlation→`r²=1`/`D'=1` (sign-blind), block oracles single→none / two-high→one / two-low→none / all-strong→one span / non-contiguous→multiple; INV `0≤r²≤1`, `0≤|D'|≤1`, block Start≤End/≥2/non-overlapping/ordered, distance+IDs preserved; edge cases empty→`r²=0,D'=0`, monomorphic (zero variance/denominator)→`r²=0` (guarded), all-identical→`r²=0`; scope = two-biallelic-loci r²/D' + adjacent-pair blocks only (no full LD matrix, no phasing/EM, no decay-curve fit, no exact Gabriel CI); no deviations/contradictions. Own concept [[linkage-disequilibrium]].
